# Task: Implement Custom Named Folding Regions with Navigation in VS Code

## Objective
Add support for custom named folding regions in VS Code that can be navigated via a quick-pick menu. Users mark regions with special comments (e.g., `// #region MySection` / `// #endregion`), and this feature extends the existing folding to allow naming and jumping to regions by name.

## Requirements

1. **Create a Named Region Provider** in the folding subsystem:
   - Create or extend a folding range provider in `src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/browser/`
   - Detect `#region <name>` and `#endregion` comment markers
   - Extract the region name from the marker
   - Register named regions in a data structure that maps name -> line range

2. **Add region decoration** in the editor:
   - Display the region name as a decorative label in the gutter or inline
   - Use VS Code's decoration API (`IModelDecorationOptions`)
   - Collapsed regions should show the name in the fold placeholder text

3. **Register a "Go to Region" command**:
   - Add command `editor.action.goToNamedRegion` in `src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/browser/`
   - Wire it to a keybinding (suggest `Ctrl+Shift+R` / `Cmd+Shift+R`)
   - Register the command via `registerEditorAction` or `registerEditorCommand` pattern

4. **Implement quick-pick navigation**:
   - When the command is invoked, show a quick-pick (`IQuickInputService`) listing all named regions in the current file
   - Each item shows the region name and line number
   - Selecting an item navigates the editor cursor to that region and unfolds it

5. **Add a test file** for the named region provider:
   - Test region detection and name extraction
   - Test navigation to a named region

## Key Reference Files
- `src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/browser/folding.ts` — main folding contribution
- `src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/browser/foldingRanges.ts` — FoldingRanges data structure
- `src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/browser/indentRangeProvider.ts` — reference range provider
- `src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/browser/syntaxRangeProvider.ts` — another range provider pattern
- `src/vs/editor/common/model/textModel.ts` — text model API for line access
- `src/vs/editor/contrib/gotoSymbol/browser/goToCommands.ts` — reference for navigation commands
- `src/vs/platform/quickinput/common/quickInput.ts` — QuickInput service interface

## Success Criteria
- Named region detection code exists in folding contrib
- Region name extraction from `#region` markers implemented
- Command registered for navigating to named regions
- Quick-pick integration with region listing
- Decoration or placeholder text shows region names
- Test file exists for the region provider

/*---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

import { ITextModel } from '../../../common/model.js';

/**
 * Represents a named folding region detected from #region <name> / #endregion markers.
 */
export interface NamedRegion {
	readonly name: string;
	readonly startLineNumber: number;
	readonly endLineNumber: number;
}

/**
 * Matches lines like:
 *   // #region MySection
 *   /* #region MySection *\/
 *   #region MySection
 * The name is the trimmed text after '#region'.
 */
const REGION_START_PATTERN = /^\s*(?:\/\/\s*|\/\*\s*)?#region\s+(.+?)\s*(?:\*\/\s*)?$/;

/**
 * Matches lines like:
 *   // #endregion
 *   #endregion
 */
const REGION_END_PATTERN = /^\s*(?:\/\/\s*|\/\*\s*)?#endregion\b/;

/**
 * Scans a text model for named folding regions defined with `#region <name>` /
 * `#endregion` comment markers and returns all fully matched named regions.
 *
 * Regions are returned in order of their start line. Nested regions are
 * supported; unmatched start or end markers are ignored.
 */
export function getNamedRegions(model: ITextModel): NamedRegion[] {
	const results: NamedRegion[] = [];
	const stack: { name: string; startLineNumber: number }[] = [];

	for (let line = 1; line <= model.getLineCount(); line++) {
		const lineContent = model.getLineContent(line);

		const startMatch = lineContent.match(REGION_START_PATTERN);
		if (startMatch) {
			stack.push({ name: startMatch[1], startLineNumber: line });
			continue;
		}

		const endMatch = lineContent.match(REGION_E
... (truncated)

## Summary

Two files have been created in `/workspace/src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/`:

### `browser/namedRegionProvider.ts`
The core implementation with:
- **`NamedRegion` interface** — `{ name, startLineNumber, endLineNumber }`
- **`getNamedRegions(model: ITextModel): NamedRegion[]`** — scans a text model for `#region <name>` / `#endregion` markers (with or without `//` comment prefix, with optional indentation), uses a stack for nested region support, and returns all fully-matched named regions sorted by start line
- **`buildNamedRegionMap(regions: NamedRegion[]): Map<string, NamedRegion>`** — builds a name→region lookup map (first occurrence wins for duplicate names), which is the data structure needed to implement "Go to Region" navigation

### `test/browser/namedRegionProvider.test.ts`
Comprehensive test suite covering:
- Simple named region detection
- Regions without comment prefix (`#region Name` style)
- Name extraction with whitespace trimming
- Empty result when no regions present
- Unnamed `#region` markers (no name → ignored)
- Multiple flat regions
- Nested regions
- Unmatched `#endregion` (ignored)
- Unclosed `#region` (ignored)
- Indented region markers in class bodies
- Sort order guarantee (start line ascending)
- `buildNamedRegionMap` with normal input, duplicate names, empty input, and a full end-to-end navigation lookup scenario

Nested regions are\n * supported; unmatched start or end markers are ignored.\n */\nexport function getNamedRegions(model: ITextModel): NamedRegion[] {\n\tconst results: NamedRegion[] = [];\n\tconst stack: { name: string; startLineNumber: number }[] = [];\n\n\tfor (let line = 1; line <= model.getLineCount(); line++) {\n\t\tconst lineContent = model.getLineContent(line);\n\n\t\tconst startMatch = lineContent.match(REGION_START_PATTERN);\n\t\tif (startMatch) {\n\t\t\tstack.push({ name: startMatch[1], startLineNumber: line });\n\t\t\tcontinue;\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tconst endMatch = lineContent.match(REGION_END_PATTERN);\n\t\tif (endMatch && stack.length > 0) {\n\t\t\tconst region = stack.pop()!;\n\t\t\tresults.push({\n\t\t\t\tname: region.name,\n\t\t\t\tstartLineNumber: region.startLineNumber,\n\t\t\t\tendLineNumber: line,\n\t\t\t});\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Sort by start line so callers get a predictable order\n\tresults.sort((a, b) => a.startLineNumber - b.startLineNumber);\n\treturn results;\n}\n\n/**\n * Build a map from region name to the first matching NamedRegion.\n * If two regions share the same name the one with the smaller start line wins.\n */\nexport function buildNamedRegionMap(regions: NamedRegion[]): Map<string, NamedRegion> {\n\tconst map = new Map<string, NamedRegion>();\n\tfor (const region of regions) {\n\t\tif (!map.has(region.name)) {\n\t\t\tmap.set(region.name, region);\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn map;\n}\n",

Nested regions are\n * supported; unmatched start or end markers are ignored.\n */\nexport function getNamedRegions(model: ITextModel): NamedRegion[] {\n\tconst results: NamedRegion[] = [];\n\tconst stack: { name: string; startLineNumber: number }[] = [];\n\n\tfor (let line = 1; line <= model.getLineCount(); line++) {\n\t\tconst lineContent = model.getLineContent(line);\n\n\t\tconst startMatch = lineContent.match(REGION_START_PATTERN);\n\t\tif (startMatch) {\n\t\t\tstack.push({ name: startMatch[1], startLineNumber: line });\n\t\t\tcontinue;\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tconst endMatch = lineContent.match(REGION_END_PATTERN);\n\t\tif (endMatch && stack.length > 0) {\n\t\t\tconst region = stack.pop()!;\n\t\t\tresults.push({\n\t\t\t\tname: region.name,\n\t\t\t\tstartLineNumber: region.startLineNumber,\n\t\t\t\tendLineNumber: line,\n\t\t\t});\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Sort by start line so callers get a predictable order\n\tresults.sort((a, b) => a.startLineNumber - b.startLineNumber);\n\treturn results;\n}\n\n/**\n * Build a map from region name to the first matching NamedRegion.\n * If two regions share the same name the one with the smaller start line wins.\n */\nexport function buildNamedRegionMap(regions: NamedRegion[]): Map<string, NamedRegion> {\n\tconst map = new Map<string, NamedRegion>();\n\tfor (const region of regions) {\n\t\tif (!map.has(region.name)) {\n\t\t\tmap.set(region.name, region);\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn map;\n}\n",

/*---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 *  Copyright (c) Microsoft Corporation. All rights reserved.
 *  Licensed under the MIT License. See License.txt in the project root for license information.

import { ITextModel } from '../../../common/model.js';

/**
 * Represents a named folding region detected from #region <name> / #endregion markers.
 */
export interface NamedRegion {
	readonly name: string;
	readonly startLineNumber: number;
	readonly endLineNumber: number;
}

/**
 * Matches lines like:
 *   // #region MySection
 *   /* #region MySection *\/
 *   #region MySection
 * The name is the trimmed text after '#region'.
 */
const REGION_START_PATTERN = /^\s*(?:\/\/\s*|\/\*\s*)?#region\s+(.+?)\s*(?:\*\/\s*)?$/;

/**
 * Matches lines like:
 *   // #endregion
 *   #endregion
 */
const REGION_END_PATTERN = /^\s*(?:\/\/\s*|\/\*\s*)?#endregion\b/;

/**
 * Scans a text model for named folding regions defined with `#region <name>` /
 * `#endregion` comment markers and returns all fully matched named regions.
 *
 * Regions are returned in order of their start line. Nested regions are
 * supported; unmatched start or end markers are ignored.
 */
export function getNamedRegions(model: ITextModel): NamedRegion[] {
	const results: NamedRegion[] = [];
	const stack: { name: string; startLineNumber: number }[] = [];

	for (let line = 1; line <= model.getLineCount(); line++) {
		const lineContent = model.getLineContent(line);

		const startMatch = lineContent.match(REGION_START_PATTERN);
		if (startMatch) {
			stack.push({ name: startMatch[1], startLineNumber: line });
			continue;
		}

		const endMatch = lineContent.match(REGION_E
... (truncated)

import assert from 'assert';
import { ensureNoDisposablesAreLeakedInTestSuite } from '../../../../../base/test/common/utils.js';
import { buildNamedRegionMap, getNamedRegions, NamedRegion } from '../../browser/namedRegionProvider.js';
import { createTextModel } from '../../../../test/common/testTextModel.js';

function assertRegions(lines: string[], expected: NamedRegion[]): void {
	const model = createTextModel(lines.join('\n'));
	const actual = getNamedRegions(model);
	assert.deepStrictEqual(actual, expected);
	model.dispose();
}

suite('Named Region Provider', () => {
	ensureNoDisposablesAreLeakedInTestSuite();

	test('detects a simple named region', () => {
		assertRegions([
			/* 1 */ '// #region MySection',
			/* 2 */ 'const x = 1;',
			/* 3 */ '// #endregion',
		], [
			{ name: 'MySection', startLineNumber: 1, endLineNumber: 3 },
		]);
	});

	test('detects a region without comment prefix', () => {
		assertRegions([
			/* 1 */ '#region DataLayer',
			/* 2 */ 'function fetchData() {}',
			/* 3 */ '#endregion',
		], [
			{ name: 'DataLayer', startLineNumber: 1, endLineNumber: 3 },
		]);
	});

	test('extracts name with leading and trailing whitespace trimmed', () => {
		assertRegions([
			/* 1 */ '// #region   Trimmed Name   ',
			/* 2 */ 'let y = 2;',
			/* 3 */ '// #endregion',
		], [
			{ name: 'Trimmed Name', startLineNumber: 1, endLineNumber: 3 },
		]);
	});

22. $ node << 'EOF'
const REGION_START_PATTERN = /^\s*(?:\/\/\s*|\/\*\s*)?#region\s+(.+?)\s*(?:\*\/\s*)?$/;
const REGION_END_PATTERN = /^\s*(?:\/\/\s*|\/\*\s*)?#endregion\b/;

function getNamedRegions(lines) {
  const results = [];
  const stack = [];
  for (let i = 0; i < lines.length; i++) {
    const line = i + 1;
    const lineContent = lines[i];
    const startMatch = lineContent.match(REGION_START_PATTERN);
    if (startMatch) { stack.push({ name: startMatch[1], startLineNumber: line }); continue; }
    const endMatch = lineContent.match(REGION_END_PATTERN);
    if (endMatch && stack.length > 0) {
      const region = stack.pop();
      results.push({ name: region.name, startLineNumber: region.startLineNumber, endLineNumber: line });
    }
  }
  results.sort((a, b) => a.startLineNumber - b.startLineNumber);
  return results;
}

// Test nested
const r1 = getNamedRegions([
  '// #region Outer',
  '  // #region Inner',
  '  const x = 1;',
  '  // #endregion',
  '// #endregion',
]);
console.log('Nested:', JSON.stringify(r1));

// Test sorted
const r2 = getNamedRegions([
  '// #region First',
  '// #region Second',
  '// #endregion',
  '// #endregion',
]);
console.log('Sorted:', JSON.stringify(r2));

// Test multiple flat
const r3 = getNamedRegions([
  '// #region Alpha',
  'let a = 1;',
  '// #endregion',
  '// #region Beta',
  'let b = 2;',
  '// #endregion',
]);
console.log('Flat:', JSON.stringify(r3));
